  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText16235224392839934726" style="display:none">Gideon calls me his angel, but he’s the miracle in my life. My gorgeous, wounded warrior, so determined to slay my demons while refusing to face his own.<br /><br />The vows we’d exchanged should have bound us tighter than blood and flesh. Instead they opened old wounds, exposed pain and insecurities, and lured bitter enemies out of the shadows. I felt him slipping from my grasp, my greatest fears becoming my reality, my love tested in ways I wasn’t sure I was strong enough to bear.<br /><br />At the brightest time in our lives, the darkness of his past encroached and threatened everything we’d worked so hard for. We faced a terrible choice: the familiar safety of the lives we’d had before each other or the fight for a future that suddenly seemed an impossible and hopeless dream.…</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">from Sylvia's FAQ: "To avoid what happened with the shuffling of Entwined with You’s release date, we’re going to refrain from announcing a date until<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">from Sylvia's FAQ: "To avoid what happened with the shuffling of Entwined with You’s release date, we’re going to refrain from announcing a date until the book is in production and everything is Set. In. Stone. You’ve seen something like this recently with the release of Dan Brown’s Inferno–it was announced in mid-January and in readers’ hands mid-May." Also, it looks like she's on tour in Brazil from the end of August through the beginning of September, so I'm guessing she's tied up for a few weeks more anyway.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<div id="review_631684992" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/631684992" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/631684992?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer631684992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5042316991921304966"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 5 STARS!!! :::: </b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416378531i/11945423.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374913i/729280._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>My casting for Gideon & Eva ^^^</i><br/><br/><b>SQUEEE!!! I absolutely LOVED this book!! </b><br/><br/>I love this series. I love these characters. I love the writing. I love the story. I love the intensity of Gideon and Eva's love for each other. I love their passion. I love the character development. I've loved everything about the Crossfire series from the very beginning and this was another fantastic addition!! 5 STARS!!<br/><br/>This is the fourth book in this series and continues Gi</span>
  <span id="freeText5042316991921304966" style="display:none"><b> ::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 5 STARS!!! :::: </b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416378531i/11945423.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374913i/729280._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>My casting for Gideon &amp; Eva ^^^</i><br><br><b>SQUEEE!!! I absolutely LOVED this book!! </b><br><br>I love this series. I love these characters. I love the writing. I love the story. I love the intensity of Gideon and Eva's love for each other. I love their passion. I love the character development. I've loved everything about the Crossfire series from the very beginning and this was another fantastic addition!! 5 STARS!!<br><br>This is the fourth book in this series and continues Gideon and Eva's story than began in Bared To You. In order to prevent spoilers, I'm not going to discuss the plot at all, just my feelings about this book so you're perfectly safe to read this review even if you haven't yet read the book. -- NO SPOILERS HERE!!<br><br>Gideon and Eva's relationship is one I feel for so strongly. I love their dynamic -- these two damaged souls, who both make their fair share of mistakes, but who love each other with every fiber of their beings, more than anything else in the world, and that love gives them the strength and courage to face their fears and work together to create a healthier and stronger relationship and future.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He buried his face in my throat. "Love you."<br>Tears stung my eyes… <br>"Tell me again," I begged, holding on to him.<br>His mouth found mine. "I love you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Having the added bonus of Gideon's POV in this book was such a thrill. The story is told in dual POV and I felt that seeing both sides of the story added so much depth at this point in the series.<br><br>When Sylvia Day first announced that this series would be extended to 5 books ages ago, my honest reaction was that, as long as she stayed true to these characters and didn't create an "drama for drama's sake" then I was quite happy that their story would continue on because quite frankly, these characters are SO complex and their relationship still has SO potential for future development that I'm thrilled to know what I'll be able to follow along every step of their journey and not have it be rushed. So far, I've loved everything that Ms. Day has written and have absolutely no complaints about any part of this series. As long as the story continues in this fashion, then I'd be happy to read even another 50 Crossfire books.<br><br>I honestly just have so much respect for the way she's handled the entire storyline of the series so far. Everything she's written has just served to strengthen the story and the characters. I love that at the core of this series is centered around the idea and effort of building a stronger relationship, not tearing it down. The angst and heart-racing intensity comes from how much you care and feel for these characters. Gideon and Eva certainly are not perfect people, but I feel like their flaws make them feel that much more real, and their love and way they support each other is absolutely beautiful.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Despite all he'd been though, he had such an amazing capacity to feel and to love. He'd saved me, in so many ways. I was going to do whatever needed to be done to save him, too."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>In every way, Captivated By You was a true Crossfire book. Even though I didn't re-read the other books before starting this, I instantly reconnected to the characters and lost myself back in their story. I read the book in one sitting and could not put it down at all. The ending is exactly the same "kind" as the first 3 books. It leaves you at a point in their relationship where things are looking up for them and you feel like they're headed in a better, stronger direction. At the same time, it leaves you eager for the next book, without leaving you hanging. I love the way these books end and have always been happy with them.<br><br>Gideon has been one of my favorite book heroes since Bared To You. I love that even though he's powerful, successful, and dominating, we are also shown his vulnerable side too. This was made even more clear through his POV. This is a man deeply scared by his past, fighting nightmares in his sleep and memories when he's awake, who has fallen desperately, passionately, all-conumingly in love with a woman who not only is the love of his life, but who also understands his pain and his past on a deep, personal level.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I told you I was going to fuck this up. I'll fuck up again. I don't know what the hell I'm doing, but God… I love you. I love you so fucking much. I can't do this without you. I can't live without you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Their path towards building a healthy relationship has never been easy but the strength of the foundation of their unwavering love for each other has given them a base to not only build up from but also to fall back on. No matter what, their love stays strong. And I love that. Theirs is a beautiful, intense, heart-wrenching journey filled with both mistakes and failures and accomplishments and progress. It's passionate, addictive, and truly one of the best I've ever read. I absolutely adore this couple, I've loved every part of their story so far, and I can't wait to see what comes next for them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You'll never be without me. We're going to grow old together. Die together. I'm not going to live a single day without you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b> Rating: 5 STARS </b><br><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5042316991921304966" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText15146555078724538994" style="display:none"><b>3 I'm being generous here... and Only Gideon Stars<br><br><i>Take me. Take all of me. The good and the bad. Everything. Take it all.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417374957ra/12317129.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, finally we are here. Almost a year and a half since book 3 we are getting more Gideon, drama Eva, drama, sex, unnecessary drama and their merry band of family, exes, friends and enemies. So lots of...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403031901ra/10027786.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Got it? Stretching the plot thin might have worked with our Gideon addiction (who sane woman with a a working pair of ovaries can ever get enough of him?) but it didn't do justice to anything else. I liked the involvement of their families in this one but it came rather late in the books to believe in it. Enemies and exes are coming vengeful out of nowhere and I feel that Gideon and Eve are fighting just on principle. Come on girl! Submit and have his babies to get over with it!<br><br>If you ask, yes I am reading the next. To drool over Gideon. But I lost my investment in these books. I no longer care and when I do the next, hopefully before my hair turn gray, I will mainly do so to criticize it. Not with malicious intent. Never. But as someone in love with the heroes I feel that I have the right to care for what is happening to them.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417374957ra/12317131.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><pre>I LOVE YOU GIDEON CROSS</pre><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910855i/3191490.jpg" width="400" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><i>Please keep reading for my pre-release rant...</i><br><br><b>2 more books in the Crossfire Series....</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/551359.gif" width="500" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Hold on a bloody minute....<br><br>2????       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✿kawehi.reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✿kawehi.reviews" href="/user/show/12789361-kawehi-reviews">✿kawehi.reviews</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer618471993" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11940626407491261870"><b>*This is just a matter of opinion guys.*</b><br/><br/>I like this series, I do. But was it just me or was being in Gideon's POV just feel a tad off? I don't know, I just felt disconnected with him.<br/><br/>Also... while you do see Ava and Gideon making progress in regards to their relationship, there was no substantial anything that occurred in this book. It just felt flat and redundant throughout.<br/><br/>*sighs* Sorry, I may be being a tad hard on this read but I didn't feel it matched up to the hype it had been given.<br/><br/>Strang</span>
  <span id="freeText11940626407491261870" style="display:none"><b>*This is just a matter of opinion guys.*</b><br /><br />I like this series, I do. But was it just me or was being in Gideon's POV just feel a tad off? I don't know, I just felt disconnected with him.<br /><br />Also... while you do see Ava and Gideon making progress in regards to their relationship, there was no substantial anything that occurred in this book. It just felt flat and redundant throughout.<br /><br />*sighs* Sorry, I may be being a tad hard on this read but I didn't feel it matched up to the hype it had been given.<br /><br />Strangely enough, <b>I DO</b> plan on reading bk5 though when it comes out. I figure, why not finish what I already started? <i>Right?</i><br /><br />Anyway, a mixed read for me.....Not wonderful, yet, not horrible either.<br /><br />THE END.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/974378510?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23172459-captivated-by-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=cheat-my-feelings">cheat-my-feelings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=imma-hit-that-bitch">imma-hit-that-bitch</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=look-at-me-giving-zero-fucks">look-at-me-giving-zero-fucks</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer974378510" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5511584981865398712"><b>ZERO FARK GIVEN STARS *RAGE MODE*</b><br/><br/><i>♥ Most epic Buddy Read with my funny ladies: Eda, Flo & Supreet! Thanks lovelies, couldn't have done this without you! ♥</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416586932ra/12007019.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In today's lesson on <b>how to ruin an initially great series</b>, here's an easy step-to-step guide. <br/><br/><b>Step 1</b>: Write a trilogy and announce at the end of the book that <b>there'll be more books to come!</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416540695ra/11992370.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Step 2:</b> Make your readers <b>wait for 1 and a half year</b> for the next book to be out.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416586932ra/12007020.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Step 3:</b> Releases said book to only find out later that it's <b>filled with non</b></span>
  <span id="freeText5511584981865398712" style="display:none"><b>ZERO FARK GIVEN STARS *RAGE MODE*</b><br><br><i>♥ Most epic Buddy Read with my funny ladies: Eda, Flo &amp; Supreet! Thanks lovelies, couldn't have done this without you! ♥</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416586932ra/12007019.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In today's lesson on <b>how to ruin an initially great series</b>, here's an easy step-to-step guide. <br><br><b>Step 1</b>: Write a trilogy and announce at the end of the book that <b>there'll be more books to come!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416540695ra/11992370.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Step 2:</b> Make your readers <b>wait for 1 and a half year</b> for the next book to be out.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416586932ra/12007020.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Step 3:</b> Releases said book to only find out later that it's <b>filled with nonsensical bored out of my freakin mind filler plot.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416576244ra/12001648.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Step 4: Charges $8</b> for said book.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416586932ra/12007020.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Step 5:</b> Ends the book by saying the next one is coming soon. <b>WELL, RINSE AND REPEAT PEOPLE.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416586932ra/12007020.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well now that's outta the way, I'm not even gonna say it's a huge disappointment because clearly, I give ZERO FARKS about this series anymore. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416588201ra/12008859.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But to sum this book up for me, basically this is what I honestly think SD felt when she wrote this book.</b><br> <br>SD: Oh dear, my readers love Gideon &amp; Eva so much, I can't let this trilogy end yet. Perhaps I should write more books and continue this series. But what else can I write about these two anymore? HMMM. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416588201ra/12008860.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>(6 months later)</i><br>SD: Oh gosh, I'm still stuck but I need to write SOMETHING soon. Perhaps I should let my readers wait a little longer.<br><br><i>(Another 6 months later)</i><br>SD: Okay they're all hounding me, I'm gonna do this! Gideon and Eva...okay I'm just gonna leave <b>them to their dysfunctional ways and have them yelling back and forth at each other</b>. Now let's throw in some jealousy, everyone <i>loves</i> a good drama. Okay <b>Corrine and Brett</b>, it's your time to shine again! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416588782ra/12009489.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>SD: What else...how about <b>some more filler scenes</b> with Cary, Gideon's mummy and stepdaddy. Family drama is always so much fun! And let's throw in Megumi too although I'm sure no one cares about her. Oh and of course, let's not forget those sex scenes! Office scene anyone?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416356762ra/11942953.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>SD: Now for some emotional scenes, get my readers to <b>ache for Gideon's awful past and his damaged self.</b> And Eva dear, let's make her a <b>crazy insecure wife that drives Gideon mad</b> because she's so damn good at it. I think my readers will love watching these two getting so frustrated at each other, it'll be so fun! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416589288ra/12009974.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>SD: Anddd voila! Now that'll satisfy my readers long enough to keep them waiting for the next one :D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And there you have it. It truly felt like the author <b>couldn't even be bothered to write a proper book</b> after making her readers wait for what seems to be an eternity. What a complete joke. The writing and plot was <b>completely half-arsed</b> and almost like <b>she wrote the book JUST BECAUSE SHE HAD TO.</b> Boring, boring and for crying out loud, <b>AWFULLY BORING.</b> <br><br>Gideon and Eva's relationship was in a <b>constant loop of insecurities</b> and basically rehashing the same old shit over and over and over again. <i>"Oh stop hurting me!" "I can't live without you!" "Let's just fight and have awesome make-up sex!"</i>. And although the descriptive sex scenes were cut down, <b>it was still all "let's just have sex everywhere because it fixes all our problems".</b> Yup, we're talking morning sex, bathroom sex, kitchen counter sex, limo sex, office sex etc AND ALL WHICH I DON'T GIVE A FLYING FARK ANYMORE. <br><br><b>This could have easily been Entwined with You 2.0 where basically it was all filler and no progression. What's new?</b> <br><br>Nothing. Nothing at all *yawns*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416590363ra/12010364.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have <b>ZERO respect</b> for this author anymore and I think I speak on behalf of all the readers that <b>felt cheated by this awful filler read</b> after making us wait for so long. And not only did she write a book that isn't worth the money we paid for, <b>she didn't even bother to thank her readers in her acknowledgements.</b> Instead she thanked her damn publishers at the end...like WTF? Are they the ones giving her sales or we are?! Smh.<br><br>So congratulations SD if you're trying to drive this series into the ground so deep under that it can never recover because you think you can earn a bucketload by playing us readers. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387207839ra/7550990.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aaaand I'm done. Sylvia Day, you have officially lost a reader forever. And for the record, I'm giving this <b>NEGATIVE 5 STARS</b> because I can #sorrynotsorry. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5511584981865398712" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_689244218" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/689244218" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/689244218?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/23591316-captivated-by-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dark-themes">dark-themes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dom-sub-bdsm">dom-sub-bdsm</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer689244218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9758694098841609968">The fourth book in the 'Crossfire' series, 'Captivated by You' proved to be a somewhat underwhelming reading experience for me. Maybe I've outgrown the billionaire Dom subgenre that became so popular after the success of 'Fifty Shades of Grey' or maybe this series is just dragging on too long to hold my interest. Whatever the reasons, this book didn't hold the appeal for me that the earlier books in the series did.<br/><br/>Gideon and Eva are back on...then off...then on again. For most of this book I fel</span>
  <span id="freeText9758694098841609968" style="display:none">The fourth book in the 'Crossfire' series, 'Captivated by You' proved to be a somewhat underwhelming reading experience for me. Maybe I've outgrown the billionaire Dom subgenre that became so popular after the success of 'Fifty Shades of Grey' or maybe this series is just dragging on too long to hold my interest. Whatever the reasons, this book didn't hold the appeal for me that the earlier books in the series did.<br /><br />Gideon and Eva are back on...then off...then on again. For most of this book I felt like they were just going in circles, rehashing the same old, tired arguments and not getting anywhere. I just feel like this book was stagnant. I was hoping that I'd see some big leaps and bounds in Gideon and Eva's relationship, but there weren't any meaningful developments until the very end.<br /><br />That being said, there were some interesting developments toward the end when Gideon's actions nearly cost him his relationship with Eva...again. I was interested to see where Gideon's new path of healing would take him, but it was hardly explored before this book ended. So, it was something...but not nearly enough to satiate me.<br /><br />Although the narrator for Gideon's voice didn't creep me out as badly this time, the narration still left much to be desired. Nothing about the narrator's voice conveyed the sexy, dominant man that is Gideon Cross to me. There was nothing appealing about his voice in this audiobook.<br /><br />Despite this book's short-comings, I will probably continue this series at some point. This series has lost much of it's luster for me. However, after reading four books, I feel too invested in this series to hang it up now. Much like I can't DNF a book, I have this compulsive need to finish a series if I've read past the first book or two. (I should probably get medication for that!) <br /><br />That being said, I can only hope that the next book is better than this one was. This book was just "okay" for me and lacked the intense appeal that the first couple of books had. Maybe it's the series...maybe it reflects a change in my tastes. Either way, this book was kind of a disappointment for me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9758694098841609968" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_755596328" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/755596328" />
    <a title="Eda**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6285155-eda"><img alt="Eda**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581410351p2/6285155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755596328?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eda**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eda**" href="/user/show/6285155-eda">Eda**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755596328" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3552502877239110934">♥ Epic Buddy Read with my lovelies <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31339793-jasmine' rel='nofollow noopener'>JASMINE</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/16349243-supreet-the-cupcake-queen' rel='nofollow noopener'>SUPREET</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7643503-flo-the-coffee-addict' rel='nofollow noopener'>FLO</a> ♥<br/><br/><b>
  <i>** 1 "<u>#NotEvenGideonCanSaveThis</u>" STAR **</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413810403ra/11565793.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When an author decides to stretch her world-famous series into 5 books and makes her fans wait for it <b>FOR 17 MONTHS</b>, you can’t help but think <i>”Whoooo! Something epic must be coming, yeah?”</i><br/><br/>Well, something epic did come my friends. Because this right here, is an <b>EPIC FAILURE</b>.<br/><br/>I’m not gonna say <i>”I’m so disappointed with this book.”</i> or something, because I had no hopes for it to be any good anyway</span>
  <span id="freeText3552502877239110934" style="display:none">♥ Epic Buddy Read with my lovelies <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/31339793-jasmine" rel="nofollow noopener">JASMINE</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/16349243-supreet-the-cupcake-queen" rel="nofollow noopener">SUPREET</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7643503-flo-the-coffee-addict" rel="nofollow noopener">FLO</a> ♥<br><br><b>
  <i>** 1 "<u>#NotEvenGideonCanSaveThis</u>" STAR **</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413810403ra/11565793.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When an author decides to stretch her world-famous series into 5 books and makes her fans wait for it <b>FOR 17 MONTHS</b>, you can’t help but think <i>”Whoooo! Something epic must be coming, yeah?”</i><br><br>Well, something epic did come my friends. Because this right here, is an <b>EPIC FAILURE</b>.<br><br>I’m not gonna say <i>”I’m so disappointed with this book.”</i> or something, because I had no hopes for it to be any good anyway. After the disastrous <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15731779.Entwined_with_You__Crossfire___3_" title="Entwined with You (Crossfire, #3) by Sylvia Day" rel="nofollow noopener">Entwined with You</a> re-read and seeing even some of my more optimistic friends not exactly loving this book, I was damn near sure I’d hate it, so I’m not surprised at all.<br><br>I’m sorry but I won’t even try to sugarcoat it: <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/19823.Sylvia_Day" title="Sylvia Day" rel="nofollow noopener">Sylvia Day</a> totally screwed us over.</b> <br><br>She just made all her fans, these people that have helped her get to where she is in her career today, pay <b>8 DOLLARS</b> for a book that is <b>BASICALLY A REPEAT OF BOOK#3</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416714ra/823388.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How is it even possible that <b>NOTHING</b> substantial happened in 368 pages? I would have enjoyed reading my 2958 pages long <i>“Harrison’s Principles of Internal Medicine”</i> textbook —which I actually will need to read for my upcoming exams. Moving on.— more than this repetitive loophole of <i>sex</i>, jealousy, pining, <i>sex</i>, ridiculous arguments, <i>sex</i>, therapy nonsense, <i>sex</i>, family drama, <i>sex</i>, filler and some more <i>sex</i>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412999473ra/11454433.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you haven’t read the book yet and plan on actually doing it later —which I wouldn’t recommend to <b>even my worst enemy</b>— you should stop reading this review right away. I am too pissed off to care about spoilers, so don’t say I didn’t warn you…<br><br><b>A.</b> <u>The ridiculous amount of drama about side characters that once again over-dominated the book</u><br><br>Dear Sylvia Day,<br><br><b>NO ONE GIVES A DAMN</b> about Megumi and Mark and Steve and Shawna and Will! I couldn’t even give a rats ass about Anne, Corinne, Christopher Jr, oh or even Ireland —who was actually kinda sweet!!<br><br>I really don't care or even like half these people!<br><br>So please…<b>PLEASE</b> stop trying to drag Gideon &amp; Eva’s story on with all this crap.<br><br><b>B.</b> <u>The extreme amount of sex I had to endure</u><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Some couples punished each other with pain or deprivation. Eva and I, we punished each other with pleasure.<br>~ GIDEON</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/580463.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am an Erotica reader, so it pains me when I say “<b>ENOUGH WITH THE SEX ALREADY!</b>”<br><br>We get it, these two need the physical proximity to survive, yeah, these two can’t breathe without each other. Sex is a necessity in their relationship, <b>WE GET IT</b>. I am SICK AND TIRED of having to re-establish this over and over again in every book! <br><br>You can’t just screw your problems away, so please <b>JUST STOP</b>.<br><br><b>C.</b> <u>Cary, the extremely dependent BFF, constantly whining and complaining ‘bout Eva ignoring him, like a 12-year-old</u><br><br>I don’t like Cary —never have, never will . What a selfish pr*ck he is! Buried deep into his own problems, he doesn’t get that Eva has a life apart from him! <br><br>Just so the precious little bisexual boy doesn’t feel <i>deserted</i>, Gideon wants Cary to move in with them to the penthouse.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413282307ra/11488586.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No words, man. No words...<br><br>Oh and how about Cary's comment about <i>”wishing Trey was bi, so that they could both be banging Tat and each other, therefore having it all”</i>?<br><br><img src="https://p.gr-assets.com/540x540/fit/hostedimages/1416585359/12005399.gif%20" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Someone should throw him under a bus. <b>STAT.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416667711ra/12031721.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>D.</b> <u>Eva, the patronizing, hypocritical, judgmental and cruel b*tch</u><br><br><b>1)</b> The way she expects Gideon to be perfectly okay with her being “confused” about Brett Kline…<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Don’t be like that. Don’t get all icy and freeze me out.”<br><br>“You’ll have to forgive me. Listening to my wife tell me she’s confused over another man doesn’t put me in a good mood.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>…but getting pissy when he comments about <i>“helping out Corinne’s confusion”</i>. She even claims that, while Gideon made that comment deliberately to hurt her, she <i>”had hurt Gideon, yes, but could sincerely say she hadn't consciously intended to do so”</i>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416667656ra/12031618.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>YEAH. RIGHT...</b><br><br><b>2)</b> Oh and let’s not forget about Eva’s reasoning for rejecting Brett Kline —the egotistical b*stard that is butthurt because of Gideon being chosen over him, and trying to destroy Eva’s marriage just to prove a point.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “I couldn’t go back to you, Brett. Not after Gideon.”<br><br>“You say that now.”<br><br>“He makes me feel like he can’t breathe without me. I couldn’t settle for less.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>So you see, she is choosing Gideon <b>NOT BECAUSE SHE LOVES HIM INSANELY</b>, but because <b>GIDEON LOVES HIM TOO MUCH</b>, therefore stroking her over-the-top ego better.<br><br>That marriage is grounded on a wonderful foundation. *sarcasm*<br><br><b>3)</b> After a very emotional talk between Gideon and Chris, Gideon is going through one of the biggest nervous breakdowns he has ever experienced, and you know what happens? While Eva is supposed to help him get better, she succeeds in making it aaaaaall about herself and Gideon ends up comforting <b>HER</b>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>G: “Yes, I was different! You made me different.”<br><br>E: “And you hate me for that.” I started crying.<br><br>G: “No.” He wrapped himself around me.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416667656ra/12031619.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>E.</b> <u>And lastly…Gideon Cross, who disappointed me more than anyone else in this awful book</u><br><br>I wish we never got to read from Gideon’s POV. Now, I have lost my only reason to bother to read this series. <b>GIDEON IS OFFICIALLY NOT ON MY TOP 5 BOOK BOYFRIENDS LIST ANYMORE.</b><br><br><i>When has Gideon turned into a pansy, frantic school-girl?</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re the reason I breathe, I can’t turn it off. I think of nothing but you. All day. Every day. Everything I do, I do with you on my mind. There’s no room for anyone else. It kills me that you have room for him.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I wouldn’t want my man to turn into this obsessive loser, that can’t even go the toilet without holding my hand. <b>Would you?</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Gideon said to me once, that he’ll live with me loving another man just as long as he had me.<br>~ EVA</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I wouldn’t want my man to be weak enough to still want me if my heart ever beat for someone else. <b>Would you?</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m sorry,” For everything. For all you’re giving up to be with me.<br>~ GIDEON</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I wouldn’t want my man to have such a low self esteem that he would constantly apologize for not being enough for me. <b>Would you?</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> I texted her constantly. Pleas for her to call me. Notes about nothing. Comments about work. And most of all, I love you. I typed them a lot. Over and over again. I didn’t want her to forget that. Whatever my faults and fuckups, everything I did or thought or felt was love for her.<br>~ GIDEON</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I wouldn’t want my man to become a dysfunctional excuse of a man every time we fight. <b>Would you?</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396428676ra/9131954.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Will Eda be reading Book#5?</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416667656ra/12031620.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lastly, here’s the one and only beautiful quote that earned the single star this book got from me:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m hanging on by a thread, Eva.”<br><br>“You don’t have to hang on. Let go. I’ll catch you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3552502877239110934" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText179981997433182152" style="display:none"><br /><b>5 *CAPTIVATED* stars</b><br /><br />It's been a while and I almost forgot how much I enjoy Sylvia Day's effortless writing! This [to me] was flawless. The story, the writing, the pace, the flow of events, everything ... <br /><br />I planned on skimming through book 3 because I didn't remember much but, as I started reading 'Captivated by You', it all came back. Very emotional and super sexy à la Sylvia, this is my favorite book in this series so far but the stage has been set for so many events that I bet grand finale would be just that - grand!<br /><br />If you are a fan of the series, I think you'll really enjoy this installment.<br /><br />Cheers!<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <a href="http://video214.com/play/vGjKNQ1B1YIpK150uCs1Qg/s/dark" rel="nofollow noopener">'Captivated by You' mini-trailer</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer17098985029590332219">Just don't know if I'm gonna read this one or not. For me, this series has lost a lot of its momentum with the release dates being so drawn out. Originally I thought it would be a trilogy and the story got dragged out over several more releases and it's kind of lost it's sparkle.<br/><br/>I have to add that I did love the first couple of books and may well need to restart the series to fully enjoy this one. It feels like years go by and we don't have a new Crossfire book!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1109031129" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14035267097897831442"><b>4 Solid Stars </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416805726i/12070277._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>Captivated by You</i> wasn't as "captivating" for me as the first three books in the series were, but I still very much enjoyed reading it. <br/><br/>I won't lie; after finishing the previous book, I was concerned there wouldn't be enough relevant story plot left to sustain two more books. I'm happy to report I was wrong. The plot remained focused on the relationship development between Gideon and Eva and didn't resort to clichéd or contrived plot devices to keep the plot moving along. Amazing,</span>
  <span id="freeText14035267097897831442" style="display:none"><b>4 Solid Stars </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416805726i/12070277._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Captivated by You</i> wasn't as "captivating" for me as the first three books in the series were, but I still very much enjoyed reading it. <br><br>I won't lie; after finishing the previous book, I was concerned there wouldn't be enough relevant story plot left to sustain two more books. I'm happy to report I was wrong. The plot remained focused on the relationship development between Gideon and Eva and didn't resort to clichéd or contrived plot devices to keep the plot moving along. Amazing, considering this is the fourth book in a romance series about <b>
  <u>one couple. </u>
</b> <br><br>As other reviewers have mentioned, this book does have a bit of a "filler" vibe, but not enough that it hinder my overall enjoyment of the story. <br><br><i>Captivated by You</i> is a well written and provocative addition to the Crossfire series. I'm glad I trusted Sylvia Day's talent as an author to continue to give me a couple worth rooting for. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14035267097897831442" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/635981702?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4227600-martina?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4227600-martina?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4227600-martina?shelf=paperback">paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4227600-martina?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4227600-martina?shelf=absolutely-delicious">absolutely-delicious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4227600-martina?shelf=hot-reads">hot-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4227600-martina?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer635981702" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10079864388293264135">I read a few of the comments bellow and I'm quite surprised. If you loved the first three books than you shouldn't have a problem with book four or five. The author feels like there's more to the story (or just doesn't want to end the success of the series) so there will be more. Nobody says that you should read it. If Entwined with you's ending is enough for you, just don't read the rest. I'm having a hard time letting go of the characters I love so I'm happy that there are going to be more boo</span>
  <span id="freeText10079864388293264135" style="display:none">I read a few of the comments bellow and I'm quite surprised. If you loved the first three books than you shouldn't have a problem with book four or five. The author feels like there's more to the story (or just doesn't want to end the success of the series) so there will be more. Nobody says that you should read it. If Entwined with you's ending is enough for you, just don't read the rest. I'm having a hard time letting go of the characters I love so I'm happy that there are going to be more books. <br />Can't wait to see what else will happen. <br /><br />EDIT 18.02.2015 <br />I read it. I LOVED it. I don't know what to do now that it's over. <br />I knew that it's going to be interesting because it's still a story about two characters I love so much and I knew that it's going to be intense because their life always is but I didn't know just how much I'll love it. <br />For the past couple of days I've been staying up late, reading only when it's dark and trying not to read it in one sitting but it was hard to stop. I was sucked into the story as I've been the last three times and it was just as amazing and just as entertaining. <br /><br />Now I don't want to give anything away but this book was more problems than solutions. I guess it was all bound to happen at some point but all the bad from Gideon's past is coming out to bite him and they already know that Eva is his soft spot. <br />This was the base of all the problems that the couple had because Eva doesn't like to be taken care of and Gideon wants to protect her from everything and anything. <br />It was quite the journey they went on this time and it was great story to read. I just don't know how to wait for the next one. <br /><br />Everyone who has been a fan so far and is hesitant to read this one, you have to understand that the story isn't finished yet. The troubles these two face everyday are making it all feel so real and I loved that about the book. It doesn't pull it's punches just because it's a fictional story and the happy ending is going to cost the characters a lot of pain and hard times. I believe that it'll all right itself in the end but I enjoy reading it so far and I can't wait for the next one.<br /><br /> </span>

<div id="review_609641390" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609641390" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/609641390?book_show_action=true">May 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609641390" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4177674963299592604"><b>4 stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/e5c47bcb-8909-4608-8914-8e9073a21f66_zps37ba4cd6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417096397i/12212239.jpg' alt=' photo e5c47bcb-8909-4608-8914-8e9073a21f66_zps37ba4cd6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I would set the world on fire to clear a path for her, if thats what it took. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/>The fourth installment of the Crossfire series wasn’t perfect, but it was still an entertaining and enjoyable read for me. It had it’s ups (ANYTHING with Gideon. Elevator. Sex swing. Cary) Then some downs (The bickering, and there were some little things towards the end that rubbed me the wrong way). I listened to the audio version of this book and I thought the narrators were awesome. They did </span>
  <span id="freeText4177674963299592604" style="display:none"><b>4 stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/e5c47bcb-8909-4608-8914-8e9073a21f66_zps37ba4cd6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417096397i/12212239.jpg" alt=" photo e5c47bcb-8909-4608-8914-8e9073a21f66_zps37ba4cd6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I would set the world on fire to clear a path for her, if thats what it took. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>The fourth installment of the Crossfire series wasn’t perfect, but it was still an entertaining and enjoyable read for me. It had it’s ups (ANYTHING with Gideon. Elevator. Sex swing. Cary) Then some downs (The bickering, and there were some little things towards the end that rubbed me the wrong way). I listened to the audio version of this book and I thought the narrators were awesome. They did a great job bringing Gideon and Eva’s story to life. <br><br>If you asked me to sum up my feelings for Mr. Cross, I would have to take a line right out of the book to do it. This describes him perfectly. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>He was complicated and sexy and damaged and perfect. </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>Gideon Cross. I can’t get enough of one of my favorite damaged men. The way he’s able to be completely alpha, powerful and domineering, yet also broken and scarred, he’s just one of my original favorites. Eva isn’t perfect. There have been times she’s annoyed me, got under my skin, but overall I do like her. I love how she’s just as crazy for Gideon as she is for him.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/55471aa1-8ac5-42f8-8b47-efceb2d0622f_zps4b694371.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417096397i/12212240.jpg" alt=" photo 55471aa1-8ac5-42f8-8b47-efceb2d0622f_zps4b694371.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The majority of this book is the couple adjusting to being a married couple. There is some drama with both of their ex’s, some drama with their friends, some drama with their jobs, and some family drama. But up till the end, not a ton of drama between them. Which I found refreshing. <br><br>This couple is trying hard to build a healthy relationship, a healthy marriage. It’s not easy. They aren’t perfect. There is going to be some bickering and conflict. Not only do they both have some major issues, but they haven’t been together very long on top of that. Some bickering and stupid choices that would have really driven me crazy in other books I kind of let slide here. Because I feel it’s realistic. Any new couple with all these issues would go through problems and have fights. That is normal. Even though they’re relationship isn’t easy and there is a lot thrown at them, they fight together. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/ef0a36d7-5dd8-4d19-980a-0e1f3956ce18_zps9015a2d2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416962533i/12140683.jpg" alt=" photo ef0a36d7-5dd8-4d19-980a-0e1f3956ce18_zps9015a2d2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Some of the drama with the ex’s I could have done without. I did like the way the story went when it came to Gideon’s family. There was a scene between him and his stepdad that brought me to tears. And I love his little sister. My favorite secondary character is and always will be Cary. He’s got a lot going on right now. I’m hoping he makes some good choices in the next book and gets his life straightened out as well. My favorite line of the book came from him, cause lets face it... it’s not only LOL funny, but very true!<br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You two are wackjobs separately, together, you’re a goddamn nut house.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Sylvia Day knows how to write sexy and she knows how to write damaged characters. Many consider this book a ‘filler’ book and I can see where they are coming from. I, however am happy that we got one solid book (that wasn’t the final book) with them married and working through their issues. I’m hoping this means the next book will have far less bickering and they will be on more solid ground. <i>Captivated by You</i> wasn’t near as strong as her first two books in the Crossfire series, but personally I liked it better than book three. <br> I’m excited to see how the final book goes and how Eva and Gideon’s story will conclude. And here’s to hoping it’s released sooner rather than later! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/aa07739b-c1bc-49ef-8be3-991e7bc5f17e_zpsff173b89.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417096397i/12212241.jpg" alt=" photo aa07739b-c1bc-49ef-8be3-991e7bc5f17e_zpsff173b89.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4177674963299592604" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_631776643" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/631776643" />
    <a title="Mysza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza"><img alt="Mysza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433922560p2/14262653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/631776643?book_show_action=true">Jun 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mysza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mysza" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza">Mysza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/21846956-captivated-by-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14262653-mysza?shelf=favorite-read">favorite-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer631776643" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6524872518104480743"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417126467i/12233432._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So, it was supposed to be a trilogy and damn, she wrote another book. Guess what? I don't give a flying fuck. No, wait, I actually do. Sylvia Day could write 10 more books about Gideon and I would still read them.<br/><br/>Ah, we had to wait for this part for almost a year and a half.... yeah, I don't care either. It's not like I didn't have wonderful books to read in between.<br/><br/>The story is being dragged just for the sake of releasing books? I say, hell yeah, keep dragging Sylvia Day because I will never ha</span>
  <span id="freeText6524872518104480743" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417126467i/12233432._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, it was supposed to be a trilogy and damn, she wrote another book. Guess what? I don't give a flying fuck. No, wait, I actually do. Sylvia Day could write 10 more books about Gideon and I would still read them.<br><br>Ah, we had to wait for this part for almost a year and a half.... yeah, I don't care either. It's not like I didn't have wonderful books to read in between.<br><br>The story is being dragged just for the sake of releasing books? I say, hell yeah, keep dragging Sylvia Day because I will never have enough of Gideon. He was first book boyfriend that I truly fell for and Crossfire series, along with FSoG, were the books that brought my love for reading back, so you can understand me being a bit sentimental here.<br><br>Gideon is still possessive, rough, alpha male, but he can also be soft and almost sappy when it comes to Eva. And how I love that about him, how I love that this reserved and introverted mogul can change for the woman he loves. He is ready to fight the whole world to keep Eva safe and he wants to do it all alone. It bothered me a bit that while trying to protect her, he kept things from her. I totally see why she would be pissed off and fight him on this, why she wanted them to act as one, because that's what the relationship is all about. And they have a lot to be worried about, there are people from their pasts lingering, trying to hurt them, to break them apart, there is their broken past, there is Gideon's family drama and his inability to open up, there is Eva's insecurity, her family and friends' problems and so much more... I get why Eva would have second thoughts about their relationship, why Gideon's obsessive love would sometimes scare her, scare that she might lose herself along the way. But I loved that in spite of the doubts, she also knows that she can't live without him and that they have to work hard to be together no matter what.<br><br>There is not much going on, true that, but this is exactly what I loved in this part. Sometimes, when there is too much drama and MCs finally solve their problems, that's it, there is HEA but I actually miss the relationship and its development between MCs. I loved that we got to see the actual relationship between those two, when they fight and make up, when they spend time with their friends and go about their daily life, when they have rough sex and make sweet love. And they do that a lot here. For real, their sex is off the charts hot, Gideon and Eva know how to tear the sheets together.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You have to stick with me. You promised. I told you I was going to fuck this up. I'll fuck up again. I don't know what the hell I'm doing, but God... I love you. I love you so fucking much. I can't do this without you. I can't live without you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>As I said before, I will read anything with Gideon in it and I am already excited for the next installment.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417126467ra/12233433.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="6524872518104480743" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1108988365" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5807831341931433011"> <b>3 Hot Stars. </b>	<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416424403ra/11962607.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay, in this fourth book the story of Eva and Gideon continues… and well, as f*cked up as ever. I won’t tell you exactly what happen not only because it is too much on too little time. But as they try to go on with their married life (while trying to keep it a secret), the media, their past and their family don’t give them a rest, and they need to find out they keep together when hits to separate them are coming from every direction. <br/><br/>I have a love/hate relationship with this ser</span>
  <span id="freeText5807831341931433011" style="display:none"> <b>3 Hot Stars. </b>	<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416424403ra/11962607.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, in this fourth book the story of Eva and Gideon continues… and well, as f*cked up as ever. I won’t tell you exactly what happen not only because it is too much on too little time. But as they try to go on with their married life (while trying to keep it a secret), the media, their past and their family don’t give them a rest, and they need to find out they keep together when hits to separate them are coming from every direction. <br><br>I have a love/hate relationship with this series. I love Gideon, but the story is dragging so much is making me losing my interest… even in him. Waiting 17 months for a book in a series isn’t good either… there’s a lot I don’t remember and I didn’t want to lose time going back to re-read. I’ve said it before: this should have been a trilogy. Now, with the amount of unnecessary drama in this book, some of it completely ridiculous, this is just a series that is taking too long to end and losing interest with each book. Or Sylvia delivers an epic ending in the next book, or not even Gideon is going to be able to save this. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 3 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development:</b> Well, Mr. Cross is a sexy beast although his “alphaness” borders the obsession. He’s the broody and broken guy we can’t help to love. Eva is annoying and stubborn as ever, although I’m happy to say she was better in this one. <br> <b>Steam: </b> HOT! <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ugh… rape, abuse, violence. Want more?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Happy for now. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1047336660?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1047336660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17127748339769898913"><b>1 I need to bleach my brain STAR</b><br/><br/><i>Disclaimer: If you like this book...STOP READING NOW!!<br/>If you happen to be a fan of the series or SD...STOP READING NOW!!<br/>I'm serious, this is going to offend and I don't want to lose my dear friends...;P</i><br/><br/><blockquote>********************************************</blockquote><br/><u>Posted before the read: </u><br/><br/><i>
  <b>BR with the most fabulous girls around...<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/2091607-most-epic-br-ever---captivated-by-you-eda-flo-supreet-jasmine' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jasmine, Supreet and Eda!</a></b>
</i><br/><br/>Not looking forward to read this particular book, but our epic BRs make everything better. So this should be at least highly ent</span>
  <span id="freeText17127748339769898913" style="display:none"><b>1 I need to bleach my brain STAR</b><br><br><i>Disclaimer: If you like this book...STOP READING NOW!!<br>If you happen to be a fan of the series or SD...STOP READING NOW!!<br>I'm serious, this is going to offend and I don't want to lose my dear friends...;P</i><br><br><blockquote>********************************************</blockquote><br><u>Posted before the read: </u><br><br><i>
  <b>BR with the most fabulous girls around...<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/2091607-most-epic-br-ever---captivated-by-you-eda-flo-supreet-jasmine" rel="nofollow noopener">Jasmine, Supreet and Eda!</a></b>
</i><br><br>Not looking forward to read this particular book, but our epic BRs make everything better. So this should be at least highly entertaining. ;D<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416571424ra/12001190.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>********************************************</blockquote><br><br><u>Posted after reading:</u><br><br><b>MY REVIEW:</b><br><br>If you know me...it was fairly predictable how I would react to <i>Captivated by you</i>, but honestly I was hoping and even praying a little that a gazillion years between publishing the last book and this one would help Ms. Day to find some actual plot. Unfortunately...no such luck. <br><br>First off...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416664482ra/12028384.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That little gif above just shows my overall reaction to everything that happens here, from start to finish. I was angry and so damn pissed off. On the one hand I'm mad at myself for actually reading; on the other hand I was so shocked and stunned how bad a book can actually be. Yes, I'm looking at you Ms. Day and yes that's a judgy look you're receiving...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416664482ra/12028385.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is no point to map out the events that follow, or even hint at what to expect when you go in, because honest to god NOTHING happens. Absolutely nothing.<br><br>Except for me getting angry at useless fights, even more useless scenes with filler friends, talking in circles and nothing substantially happening.<br><br>Now let's talk about Eva!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416664482ra/12028386.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't think I've ever had such a strong reaction to a female character in any book. I'm just going to say it...look away if you don't want to know:<br><br>She is a hypocritical-insecure-selfish bitch! And that's actually one of the nicer things I have to say about her. <br><br>For some reason she is under the impression that she can treat people with disrespect, but once they turn the tables the gloves are off. WTF? I actually felt sorry for Gideon during that particular conversation involving Brett and Corinne.<br><br>Girl, get a grip on reality and get over yourself. Also grow up and don't run away every time something doesn't work out the way you want it to and most of all get hormones under control...just one word...Brett!<br><br>But then again Gideon isn't one bit better...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416664482ra/12028387.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously, cry me a river, Gideon! Going in I was excited to see Gideon's POV...I mean after being unsatisfied with my re-read of book 1 to 3 a little change in modus operandi is the way to go, right? Yeah, didn't work.<br><br>Actually, I take that back...we learned quite a lot in the chapters written from his POV. He is whipped, dependant on bitch face Eva and whiny. OMG, I think Jasmine said it...he comes across like a girl. He was supposed to be that super-alpha-male and then we get this? No, just NO!<br><br>There goes the favourite book-boyfriend material. ;D<br><br>And together those two nut-jobs need a lot of help and probably different people in their life. My tip...RUN...and in different directions!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416664590ra/12028411.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>But the most disappointing part is that after reading this book we are back at square one...the same lurking drama and problems that have been around for two or three books are still unresolved. It's like sitting on a roundabout seeing the same conflicts, fights and scenarios replayed over and over again. And you know what the definition of insanity is, right?<br><br>Doing the same thing over and over again and expecting a different outcome...and yet it never appears.<br><br>And in the end I only have one more thing so say...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416664482ra/12028388.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am not going to read the next book. This was the limit. All I can take. Never again!<br><br>Peace out bitches!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416665765ra/12029482.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
