<div id="review_960809945" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/960809945" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/960809945?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer960809945" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10106640136237783299"><b>4 - 4.5 <i>Mr. Dark and Dangerous</i> Stars</b><br/><br/>My love for Gideon goes way back, he basically had me from this moment: <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Because I want to fuck you, Eva. I need to know what’s standing in my way, if anything.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>I remember reading that line and thinking SHIT JUST GOT REAL. I have loved Gideon since and I anxiously await every release in this series. This particular release I hunted down the paperback book just to read it a few days early…FAIL. <br/><br/>A lot of people would classify this book as filler and honestl</span>
  <span id="freeText10106640136237783299" style="display:none"><b>4 - 4.5 <i>Mr. Dark and Dangerous</i> Stars</b><br><br>My love for Gideon goes way back, he basically had me from this moment: <br><br><b>
  <i>“Because I want to fuck you, Eva. I need to know what’s standing in my way, if anything.” </i>
</b><br><br>I remember reading that line and thinking SHIT JUST GOT REAL. I have loved Gideon since and I anxiously await every release in this series. This particular release I hunted down the paperback book just to read it a few days early…FAIL. <br><br>A lot of people would classify this book as filler and honestly I have to agree, however I don’t even care. I would gladly continue reading about Gideon indefinitely. So onto the actual review of this installment.<br><br><i>Captivated by You</i> begins where things left off. Gideon and Eva are married, but as all married people know the ring and vows are not majestical things that fix your problems. Not to mention Gideon and Eva have had a whirl wind romance and things have moved very quickly. Throw in the fact that both of them have past emotional and physical abuse…it’s pretty disastrous. I think Cary said it best:<br><br><i>
  <b>"Sure. You two are whack jobs separately. Together, you’re a goddamn nut house.”</b>
</i><br><br>Sure this is probably true, but nothing worth having comes easy, and this couple is completely dedicated to making it work. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416670849i/12034450.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>While reading I was getting frustrated with the bickering, but I had to remember this is a new relationship and they are both damaged. Truthfully, I respect the fact that Day isn’t just magically fixing their problems. We read so many books that are drama, drama, drama and then the epilogue they are magically fixed - no drama, perfect couple. That isn’t realistic. So I do commend her for stay true to her characters and showing their struggles. <br><br>As always these two are burning down the house in the bedroom. This book is so damn hot! I love Gideon and Eva’s chemistry. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416670849i/12034451.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>While we didn’t get to see everything in this one, it is foreshadowed that more trouble is on the horizon. I can’t wait to see what happens next for Gideon and Eva. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416670849i/12034452.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>If you are a fan of the series, I highly recommend reading this one. </b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10106640136237783299" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1059198215" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1059198215" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1059198215?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23172459-captivated-by-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=hot-alpha-male-billionaire">hot-alpha-male-billionaire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1059198215" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer297626416176676007"><b>*****3.5 STARS*****</b><br/>{BR with Mel, Dee, Sharon, and Tiffany}<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/26bd1914199041647e75230d487ce5cc_zps8df9574d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416720330i/12048184._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 26bd1914199041647e75230d487ce5cc_zps8df9574d.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>I can't believe it took me five days to finish this book!<br/>It felt like an eternity since I had read <b>"Entwined With You"</b>. I was upset that Sylvia Day decided to make this a 5 book series, but not enough to give up on it. I was dying to get my hands on this book. <br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>I'm so very sad that this book just didn't win me over. I found it to be kind of slow for the most part. I didn't like the unnecessary drama with Brett, Corinne, and the other t</span>
  <span id="freeText297626416176676007" style="display:none"><b>*****3.5 STARS*****</b><br>{BR with Mel, Dee, Sharon, and Tiffany}<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/26bd1914199041647e75230d487ce5cc_zps8df9574d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416720330i/12048184._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 26bd1914199041647e75230d487ce5cc_zps8df9574d.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I can't believe it took me five days to finish this book!<br>It felt like an eternity since I had read <b>"Entwined With You"</b>. I was upset that Sylvia Day decided to make this a 5 book series, but not enough to give up on it. I was dying to get my hands on this book. <br><br><br><br><br>I'm so very sad that this book just didn't win me over. I found it to be kind of slow for the most part. I didn't like the unnecessary drama with Brett, Corinne, and the other two women from Gideon's past. I pretty much disliked Eva the entire time I was reading this book.<br><br><br><br>I am only rating Gideon a <b>FIVE</b>!!<br>I loved him and his passion &amp; devotion for Eva. He would do anything to make her happy and to keep her safe. My heart broke for him that he still struggles with his nightmares and that he feared his issues would eventually have Eva leaving him.<br><br><br><br>Also the sexy time scenes were <b>INCREDIBLE</b>!!!<br>It was worth the many nights of falling asleep on my couch to get to the sex swing and elevator scenes!!<br><br><br>The drama at the end had me so heartbroken for Gideon and disliking Eva even more. I think she needs a dose of her own medicine.<br><br><br>So even though I was bored to tears throughout the book, the fact that I do love Gideon and the sexy time scenes were extremely panty melting, I couldn't see rating the book below 3.5 stars.<br><br><br>What I hope for the last book is that we don't have anymore of the unnecessary drama from ex lovers. I would like to see Gideon find peace from his painful past. Hopefully Dr Peterson will help him and his mom needs to own up to being an absolute failure as a parent. I was disappointed that this book wasn't better, seeing as the author had over a year to write this one, but I am optimistic that she can turn things around with the last book!<br><br><br>I end this review with a GIF that accurately depicts how the last four nights ended up for me while trying to read this book. :)<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/tumblr_mv3l9iEe7D1shxu82o1_400_zpsoj35cxjh.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416720330ra/12048185.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mv3l9iEe7D1shxu82o1_400_zpsoj35cxjh.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17598206362297798290"><b> 1.5 Procrastination Killer stars </b><br/><br/>Okay, it takes A LOT for me to give a book anything less than 3 stars. Seriously, go to my profile and look at my stats. It's a rare thing for me. I was literally choosing to write papers for graduate school over reading this book. I finished a damn 20+ page paper in 2 days because I was avoiding reading this book.<br/><br/>My biggest issue with the book? I was bored. That's right, BORED! <br/><br/><a href='http://reactiongifs.com/?p=14432' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398870967ra/9474151.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Gideon and Eva were boring! I still kind of can't wrap my mind around this. Afte</span>
  <span id="freeText17598206362297798290" style="display:none"><b> 1.5 Procrastination Killer stars </b><br><br>Okay, it takes A LOT for me to give a book anything less than 3 stars. Seriously, go to my profile and look at my stats. It's a rare thing for me. I was literally choosing to write papers for graduate school over reading this book. I finished a damn 20+ page paper in 2 days because I was avoiding reading this book.<br><br>My biggest issue with the book? I was bored. That's right, BORED! <br><br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=14432" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398870967ra/9474151.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gideon and Eva were boring! I still kind of can't wrap my mind around this. After the whole not a trilogy controversy after the last book, I was willing to give this one a chance. But nothing happened in this book. Honestly the only real plot development was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Gideon's stepfather finding out about the abuse, the job issue and Cary telling Trey about the baby. THAT'S IT IN 350+ PAGES  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. So needless to say I am off Team 5 Books. <br><br>Will I read the next book? Probably. I've invested this much time into the series. Will I buy it like I bought this one? Hell, no. I'll be getting it from my local library. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_728995239" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/728995239" />
    <a title="Shurrn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn"><img alt="Shurrn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410564134p2/22115857.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/728995239?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=series-unfinished">series-unfinished</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-billionaires-and-executives">c-billionaires-and-executives</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-for-kindle">z-own-for-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-modern">romance-modern</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=favorite-romantic-series">favorite-romantic-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728995239" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6473681978065480754"><b>Two steps forward; three steps back</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416446294i/11968230._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>(Spoilers only if you haven't read the first 3 Books)</i><br/><br/><u>Captivated by You</u> is the perfect springboard for a finale, but didn't quite deliver the punch expected from the Crossfire series... I think it's fair to say I'm <i>Captivated</i> by Eva & Gideon's story... Due to that fact, I also think I hold Sylvia Day to a different standard than other authors. Reading is subjective that way....<br/><br/>The true strength of the Crossfire series is found in the complexity of the characters</span>
  <span id="freeText6473681978065480754" style="display:none"><b>Two steps forward; three steps back</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416446294i/11968230._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>(Spoilers only if you haven't read the first 3 Books)</i><br><br><u>Captivated by You</u> is the perfect springboard for a finale, but didn't quite deliver the punch expected from the Crossfire series... I think it's fair to say I'm <i>Captivated</i> by Eva &amp; Gideon's story... Due to that fact, I also think I hold Sylvia Day to a different standard than other authors. Reading is subjective that way....<br><br>The true strength of the Crossfire series is found in the complexity of the characters - Deeply and tragically flawed... Their struggle humanizes a tale which could easily be lost in the extravagance of a well-worn plot.<br><br><b>Stop me if you've heard this one...</b><br><br>An alpha-male billionaire with a dominant streak who seduces a reluctant and intelligent young girl.<br><br>He relentlessly pursues her with a singular focus which borders on obsession.<br><br>She's the antithesis of his usual type, and he's forced to break all his rules for her.<br><br>He doesn't feel worthy of her, he's never been in a genuine relationship, he keeps women at a safe distance. <br><br><b>He's broken...<br>Her love will heal him...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416444107ra/11967939.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know, right? I don't think I was the only reader worried about getting tangled in overused literary tropes when I picked up the first book of this series back in 2012...<br><br>I also know I wasn't alone when I became completely entranced by Eva and Gideon's whirlwind romance.<br><br>I was left with a nearly lethal book hangover from the first books. I even re-read the books in preparation for each subsequent publication... Count it out. That means I've read the first book FOUR times...<br><br>So here's an important question; will I re-read <u>Captivated by You</u> before the release of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17876897.One_with_You__Crossfire___5_" title="One with You (Crossfire, #5) by Sylvia Day" rel="nofollow noopener">One with You</a> (whenever the fuck <i>that</i> happens)? Absolutely not. There wasn't much substance here to warrant a thorough re-reading...<br><br>However, it was a delightful tease to keep me interested in Eva and Gideon.<br><br>There was a dual point-of-view element here which I found fascinating - the POV alternated between Gideon and Eva with each chapter.<br><br>All the sizzling heat I've come to expect from the Crossfire series was there in spades. And, as usual, it was an emotional roller coaster...<br><br>This is my favorite fictional, twisted, mentally unstable couple...<br><br><b>Gideon Cross</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416444107i/11967940.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He didn’t see in himself what I saw— a generous soul who wanted so much to belong to something greater than himself. He didn’t recognize what a miracle he was. When he didn’t know what to do in a given situation, he let instinct and his heart take over. Despite all he’d been through, he had such an amazing capacity to feel and to love.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Gideon has his prize - after chasing and struggling for several months, Eva is now his wife. The rest of the world might not realize that Gideon and Eva have tied the knot, but there's no mistaking that she is <i>his</i>.<br><br>Gideon Cross once stood as the unbreakable Master of the Universe. He made many enemies as he built this corporate empire. There are countless people who would love to take him down a peg or two. <br>Those who wish to see him suffer for the sins of his father... <br>Business adversaries crushed under his ambition...<br>Countless women he callously tossed aside...<br><br>For all those people, Eva Trammel now represents a long-sought weakness for Gideon. One they intend to exploit.<br><br><b>Eva Trammel</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416444107i/11967941.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>For now, Gideon and I had secrets we could share only with each other, and that kept us isolated and codependent. It wasn’t only innocence our abusers had taken away from us; they’d also taken our freedom. Even after the abuse was long over, we were still caged by the false fronts we lived behind. Still caged by lies, but in a different way.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Eva is still struggling with the fact that Gideon keeps silent about his troubles. He doesn't share the content of his nightmares. He keeps secrets, and tries to remain an island. That doesn't work for her anymore. If they're going to be married she expects an equal partnership, but Gideon can't seem to deliver.<br><br>He manipulates her with sex and silently schemes with behind the scenes tactics. Eva knows that Gideon does this with the most honorable of intentions, but is the result really worth the emotional turmoil he repeatedly puts her through?<br><br>Still, Eva is hopelessly dependent on her emotional connection to Gideon. <br><br>He loves her deeply...<br>He has killed for her... <br>He tries so hard to make her happy and keep her safe...<br>He continues to work diligently to destroy all threats against her...<br><br>Those threats came out of the woodwork for this installment of the Crossfire series. Even though Eva's abuser is dead, ghosts from both Eva and Gideon's pasts line the streets of New York City waiting to strike them down.<br><br><b>Side Note:</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416450298ra/11968774.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cary's presence was a highlight of this book. He is struggling through some difficult situations of his own - he's caught in a love triangle between the man he loves and a woman he accidentally got pregnant - but his raw honesty with his best friend was wonderful to read. As always, the scenes with Cary infused a much-needed element of humor into this emotional book. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"...Love should be easier than this,” I complained. <br><br>“If this were a romantic comedy, it’d be called <u>Love Actually Sucks</u>.” <br><br>“Maybe we should’ve stuck with <u>Sex and the City</u>.” <br><br>“Tried that. Ended up <u>Knocked Up</u>. I should’ve gone for being a <u>40-Year-Old Virgin</u>, but I had way too much of a head start.” <br><br>“We can write a manual on How to Lose a Guy in 10 Weeks.” <br><br>Cary looked at me. “Fucking perfect.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Scenes like that were reminiscent of the classic 'Fortune Cookie' scene from book one and reminded me why I love this series.<br><br>As I said before, it's fair to say that I hold Sylvia Day to a different standard. She has already earned my loyalty to this fabulous series... <br><br>When a series encompasses a single narrative I tend to judge it based on the whole rather than the individual books. With that in mind, I feel that <u>Captivated by You</u> is merely the calm (relatively) before the storm. A bit washed out in comparison to the vibrancy of the prior books.<br><br><b>Was this an entertaining read?</b> <br>Yes.<br><b>Did the writing quality live up to my expectations?</b> <br>Absolutely.<br><b>Was I sucked in immediately?</b> <br>Hell yes.<br><b>Was this book worth the wait?</b><br>No. <br><b>Will I continue this series when the next book goes live?</b><br>You bet your ass.<br><br>I look forward to seeing what Sylvia Day has in store for us next with this series.<br><br><b>Aaaaaand now we begin the arduous wait for the fifth book...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412607017ra/11395766.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You can tell yourself that Eva and I are incompatible," I said tightly, "That we're either fighting or fucking with nothing of substance in between. But the truth is that she's the other half of me..."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> If you'd like to test this book out before you buy it, you can read the FIRST THREE CHAPTERS ON <a href="http://www.sylviaday.com/captivated-chapters/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sylvia Day's Website</a> for FREE!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6473681978065480754" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_609662173" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609662173" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/609662173?book_show_action=true">May 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609662173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17504984529480447910">I LOVE Gideon! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416616630i/12017711.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The Crossfire series is special to me in so many ways. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13572249.Bared_to_You__Crossfire___1_' title='Bared to You (Crossfire, #1) by Sylvia Day' rel='nofollow noopener'>Bared to You</a>, (Crossfire #1) is the very first book I experienced on my beloved kindle and I've never looked back. It was originally planned as 3 books but, luckily for us, Gideon took on a life of his own, he's adored by so many and this author decided to breathe life into a larger series. FIVE books! I will take as much Gideon and Eva as I'm offered. For me their story is effortless reading. It's beautiful, erotic and sensua</span>
  <span id="freeText17504984529480447910" style="display:none">I LOVE Gideon! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416616630i/12017711.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Crossfire series is special to me in so many ways. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13572249.Bared_to_You__Crossfire___1_" title="Bared to You (Crossfire, #1) by Sylvia Day" rel="nofollow noopener">Bared to You</a>, (Crossfire #1) is the very first book I experienced on my beloved kindle and I've never looked back. It was originally planned as 3 books but, luckily for us, Gideon took on a life of his own, he's adored by so many and this author decided to breathe life into a larger series. FIVE books! I will take as much Gideon and Eva as I'm offered. For me their story is effortless reading. It's beautiful, erotic and sensual. Their love affair is carried out with fierce conviction and heart breaking vulnerability. <i>They will be forever in my book heart.</i><br><br>It’s been quite some time since the last Crossfire episode but fear not reader, if you're a lover of Gideon and Eva you’ll easily remember plot points with Sylvia Day's well placed reminders about previous events and characters. <br><br><b>Captivated by You</b> is the continuation of Eva and Gideon’s romance. Their delicious, and highly erotic, sexcapades. Their trials, tribulations, inner turmoil and struggles. Their saga is one that I cherish like one would a meeting with old friends. It doesn’t need to be dramatic or highly angst ridden because a simple sentence, a reference makes me feel so much.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417036869i/12179936.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gideon said things that made me well up with emotion. We clearly see the pain of his life and it made my heart ache for him…. <i>And my tears fell. </i><br><br>I love Gideon's developing relationship with his sister, one which Eva helps to nurture. Indeed, all the supporting characters add to the mix perfectly.<br><br><b>Eva is his everything.<br><br>Gideon is her all. </b><br><br>I love getting the point of view from both Gideon and Eva. His voice is delectable his words.... <i>divine.</i> Gideon described through the eyes of Eva is wondrous. They are a match made in heaven for readers of erotic romance and I LOVE them. Eva's heart pours into her descriptions and thoughts providing us with such a clear picture of Gideon and her love for him. <br><br>They are gloriously flawed characters. Those flaws bring them together but could equally tear them apart. Their vulnerabilities have the power to feel like open wounds…. <i>Is their love for each other strong enough to overcome anything? </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417036822i/12179887.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>So HOT! </i>
</b><br><br>Sylvia day really is the epitome of erotic writing. Sex has restoring power for them, it’s a cure all ointment that's intensely passionate and HOT as sin. I love how they can completely wind each other up, irritate the hell out of each other, and then come back together with healing sex. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417034237i/12177997.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With <b>Captivated by You</b> I very much feel like I'm reading a serial drama….. That comforting feel-nice-inside-vibe. Seeing your favourite characters in various scenarios, going through different things. Think of every beautiful word and description and times by a million to have an understanding of the way I feel about these characters and the wonderful way in which this author presents them to us. I feel very much that Captivated by You leads us down a certain future path and I really hope my thoughts are realised..… I want to see the magical <i>‘Gideva’</i> fairy tale continue to thrive and be the glorious spectacle of love, hope and courage that I’ve become so very fond of.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417038391i/12180592.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will NEVER tire of reading about Gideon and Eva together. Their trials and tribulations <i>rock my world!</i><br><br><br>♥ BR with Deanna PinkLady, Irene and TeriLyn </span>
  <a data-text-id="17504984529480447910" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer609611729" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1647031310616235182"><b>5 ANGEL MINE STARS</b><br/><br/>OK so I have seen many reviews and lots of frustrations about this book. YES, it took forever and a day to get here...YES it had a lot of questions to answer...YES, it had a lot of hype...for many it did not satisfy many of their needs or wants from the series.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416537498ra/11991961.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>But GUESS WHAT? I don't give a flying hoot! I flipping loved the book! Start to Finish, I could not get enough of what Sylvia Day was laying down.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416537498i/11991962._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have followed the tumultuous relationship of Eva Trammell and Gideon Cro</span>
  <span id="freeText1647031310616235182" style="display:none"><b>5 ANGEL MINE STARS</b><br><br>OK so I have seen many reviews and lots of frustrations about this book. YES, it took forever and a day to get here...YES it had a lot of questions to answer...YES, it had a lot of hype...for many it did not satisfy many of their needs or wants from the series.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416537498ra/11991961.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But GUESS WHAT? I don't give a flying hoot! I flipping loved the book! Start to Finish, I could not get enough of what Sylvia Day was laying down.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416537498i/11991962._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have followed the tumultuous relationship of Eva Trammell and Gideon Cross from inception in <i>Bared to You</i> until now and I could not be happier. I have many questions as to the future, and I have many scenarios in the my mind that still need worked out. But for me, this book was more about the relationship of Gideon and Eva. We all know is was fast and furious full of fight and F***! Gideon Cross is a hard nut to crack...dominant, powerful, and possessive. He is also manipulative, smart, and pushy. What I love the most though is that he is a man in hard LOVE.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416537603i/11991972.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416537498ra/11991964.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have no shame in saying Gideon is quite possibly my all time Favorite "damaged male." My love for this book lies in the deeper emotions I finally got from this man. He is so deeply into Eva it is as if his next breath depends on her. As he says, it is so much more than LOVE. From his primal lust and libido that she drives, to the simple flirty smiles and relaxed cuddles he has evolved so much. Sylvia Day literally breaks him down in this book and gets to the heart of his soul...with tears, fear, and courage Gideon and Eva are making it ever so slowly and doing it the only way they know how...with ridiculous kindle melting HEAT and PASSION!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416537498ra/11991965.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know there are many loose ends still open...especially with the crazy that went down at the conclusion of book 3. I know that many new threats to their happiness were laid out. It seems as if there are miles to go before they can just "BE." People wonder why Sylvia Day is bringing MORE books...I just don't care. I got 300 some pages of Gideon Cross...300 more would be welcome and read over and over and over again! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416537498ra/11991966.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer780459212" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11422334913844446562"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You okay, angel mine?”<br/>“I’m in your arms. Life doesn’t get better than this.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>It will come as no surprise to anyone who knows me as a reader that the Crossfire series is my own personal kryptonite. No other series has kept me as emotionally invested for such a long time as these books have, having re-read each one of them countless times and always discovering new layers to the story, new details that I might have missed or skimmed over on that first…or tenth…or twentieth re-read. Thi</span>
  <span id="freeText11422334913844446562" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You okay, angel mine?”<br>“I’m in your arms. Life doesn’t get better than this.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>It will come as no surprise to anyone who knows me as a reader that the Crossfire series is my own personal kryptonite. No other series has kept me as emotionally invested for such a long time as these books have, having re-read each one of them countless times and always discovering new layers to the story, new details that I might have missed or skimmed over on that first…or tenth…or twentieth re-read. This is one of the most powerful, passionate love stories that I know of, Gideon and Eva being two such meticulously developed characters that we cannot help but want to talk about them over and over again, psychoanalysing their every action, their every word, their every breath, because they feel that real to us. This fourth instalment in the series is possibly my favourite of the lot, encompassing every single element I hoped to find in it, in particular the careful attention that is paid to these characters’ emotional growth and change. There was not a moment that I did not understand the motivation behind their actions and reactions, and there was not one scene that did not make my heart race or skip a beat. Every word in it counts, every emotionally charged scene plays a vital role in the overall storyline, and every part of the puzzle is fundamental to our deeper understanding of the key players in it. This book was everything I wished it would be, and so much more, my mind still reeling from the mere brilliance of the way these characters are brought to life. Bravo, Ms Day!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Are you in love, Mr. Cross?”<br>“Irrevocably.”</i>
</blockquote><br>They may have known each other for just a few months, but Eva and Gideon’s tumultuous relationship has survived through enough trials to last them a lifetime. But even after exchanging vows in secret and promising their forevers to one another, they know that there are still many obstacles before them, most of them stemming from Gideon’s past and the painful memories he refuses to address. Their unique connection is their biggest strength—their almost visceral bond and need for each other being their greatest weapon against the world that questions their commitment to one another and tries to pull them apart—but that connection is also their greatest weakness as it isolates them from others, making them codependent and essential for each other’s happiness. As we finally hear Gideon’s voice in this book, we get to see firsthand the depth of his love for Eva and how her presence in his life has changed him. Her unwavering devotion, her protectiveness of him, and her every touch silence the demons that devastate him through his dreams and affect his every human connection.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You’re the reason I breathe, I can’t turn it off. I think of nothing but you. All day. Every day. Everything I do, I do with you in mind. There’s no room for anyone else.”</i>
</blockquote><br>As the limelight is put on the their young relationship, their private moments in each other’s arms are what drives that relationship forward, their intimacy with one another growing with each sexual encounter, every kiss, every embrace. Behind closed doors, they are one, both physically as well as mentally, completely in sync and vulnerable only to one another. They understand the other person’s needs and addictions better than anyone else in their lives, their frequent and very intense lovemaking sessions sustaining and temporarily satiating their hunger for one another. No part of themselves is hidden, no sexual act is off limits, and their physical as well as emotional addiction to each other only grows. And within their unique dynamic, sex still remains their primary mode of communication.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“She was every promise, every hope, every fantasy a man could have. And she was mine.”</i>
</blockquote><br>But as they work on improving themselves in order to have a functional and healthy relationship with each other, old foes from Gideon’s past keep resurfacing, relentlessly set on destroying him and making him pay for his past sins. For the first time in his adult life, he has shown the world his only weakness—Eva—and they are willing to hurt her in order to get to him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“She’s the chink in your armor, you heartless piece of shit. You’ve got ice in your veins, but she bleeds … It’s time to pay, and your billions won’t cover the debt.”</i>
</blockquote><br>We watch our fearless hero battle his past, fight for a future with the woman he loves, all along navigating through marital waters he never imagined himself embarking upon. Nothing in their marriage is left to chance, their every energy dedicated to honouring their commitment to one another, to being what the other needs, craves, wants, and to shouldering each other’s burdens. But every step comes with a hurdle, every achievement with a mistake, and every lesson learned with a hefty price attached to it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I would set the world on fire to clear a path for her, if that’s what it took.”</i>
</blockquote><br>There is an extraordinary self-awareness present in these characters that makes them incredibly fascinating to watch, overcoming their personal hang-ups being their greatest challenge both personally as well as a couple. I was enthralled start to finish, reading slowly in order to absorb every emotion, swallow every word. Ms Day’s writing style is unmatched, her confident and sophisticated prose pulling us in and making us feel every emotion she wishes us to feel. I walked away emotionally drained, with the biggest smile on my face, thrilled for everything that my two favourite characters achieved in such a short time span, but more than happy to wait for their grand finale as their story concludes in the next book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’m hanging on by a thread, Eva.”<br>“You don’t have to hang on. Let go. I’ll catch you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380382869i/740934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2014/11/20/captivated-by-you-sylvia-day/" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a> | <a href="http://www.twitter.com/natashabkjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Twitter!</a><br><br>Amazon US: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1s3AybC">http://amzn.to/1s3AybC</a><br>Amazon UK: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1oQQHLK">http://amzn.to/1oQQHLK</a><br>Amazon CA: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1rTCjdq">http://amzn.to/1rTCjdq</a><br>Paperback: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1qzPkGw">http://amzn.to/1qzPkGw</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11422334913844446562" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1109754773" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1109754773" />
    <a title="Gail - Slitty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14970042-gail---slitty"><img alt="Gail - Slitty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379782583p2/14970042.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1109754773?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gail - Slitty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gail - Slitty" href="/user/show/14970042-gail---slitty">Gail - Slitty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1109754773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1292494060221006591">***Possible Spoiler Alert-(whispers "although nothing new happens")<br/><br/>*Yawn* Was there a purpose to this book? Unless the purpose behind this book was an attempt at driving this series into the ground, then congratulations, it was a success. This book is similar to ordering a box of candies from a company that you’ve trusted in the past, and they send you a huge box, and you think that it’s going to be filled with all sorts of goodness, but then you open the box, and it’s filled with nothing but pa</span>
  <span id="freeText1292494060221006591" style="display:none">***Possible Spoiler Alert-(whispers "although nothing new happens")<br /><br />*Yawn* Was there a purpose to this book? Unless the purpose behind this book was an attempt at driving this series into the ground, then congratulations, it was a success. This book is similar to ordering a box of candies from a company that you’ve trusted in the past, and they send you a huge box, and you think that it’s going to be filled with all sorts of goodness, but then you open the box, and it’s filled with nothing but packing peanuts, and you keep searching thinking that you’re going to find something, and finally after going through all the packaging, you find a caramel. The packing peanuts in this book are the sex scenes, and try as you may to search through all of them, but you aren’t going to find a caramel, maybe a piece of butterscotch candy. Because I enjoy erotica, it pains me to say “Enough with the sex”, please, we get it, we also get that they need each other to survive, Gideon is the yin to Eva’s yang, he can’t breathe without her, his body hurts not being inside her, they feel each other’s presence before they see each other, their skin aches when they part, WE GET THIS, IT WAS ESTABLISHED OVER AND OVER AND OVER AND OVER AND OVER AND OVER IN ALL THREE PREVIOUS BOOKS. Seriously, they have sex before work, while on the way to work, while at work, and then after work, at this point I would be happy just to see either one standing at the water cooler talking to a co-worker about the last episode of The Walking Dead, fucking anything but the two of them fucking. It would be nice to read one of having an independent scene without the other waiting in the shadows. It would be interesting to see Eva going to California without Gideon trailing, as it would to read about Eva going to lunch without Gideon waiting a table close-by, it would have been interesting to read any scene without them together, because as we all find out, they can’t be together without engaging in sex. That’s is all there is to this book is the sex, and although I like sex scenes, it would be nice to have a little storyline to go along with it. I skipped through dozens of pages because the sex is a yawn fest. <br /> <br />This series began with beautiful, wealthy, interesting yet flawed and damaged people. It has turned into a series about beautiful co-dependents that I seriously doubt can take a piss without the other one holding his/her hand. I now loathe Cary, instead of him being a supporter and friend to Eva, all he thinks about is how her every move is going to impact him. This book is essentially the three of them having sex, making each other miserable, whining and complaining, but can’t be away from each other for longer than an hour. C’mon, how ridiculous is it that Gideon wants Cary to move in the penthouse that he and Eva are having remodeled so that Cary doesn’t feel deserted. Gideon has turned into a pansy, frantic schoolgirl, but instead of passing notes of “Do you like me, yes or no?”, he sends texts. Corrine having sex with Angus would be more interesting than to reading this, watching paint dry on the walls would be more interesting than this. <br /> <br />As with book three (Entwined with You) in this series, nothing was resolved, nothing new occurred, it was basically a repeat of book three. The name of this book should have been: Entwined with You Version 2.0, or Gideon Fucks Eva Again and Again and Again and Again and Again and Again and Again and Again. <br /><br />Save your money folks, nothing new going on here. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1292494060221006591" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_609679234" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609679234" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/609679234?book_show_action=true">May 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609679234" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15215193831317909608">Gideon & Ava’s story continues in part four of this series. Returning to the real world, secretly married but having to keep it under wraps. As news of their engagement breaks, these two navigate planning a future while Ava is trying to help Gideon put the past to rest. <br/><br/>I know that there are a lot of readers out there that were upset about the expansion of the trilogy to five books and the timeframe of the release, but for me, that never mattered. Sure I wanted the book sooner – but having to wa</span>
  <span id="freeText15215193831317909608" style="display:none">Gideon &amp; Ava’s story continues in part four of this series. Returning to the real world, secretly married but having to keep it under wraps. As news of their engagement breaks, these two navigate planning a future while Ava is trying to help Gideon put the past to rest. <br><br>I know that there are a lot of readers out there that were upset about the expansion of the trilogy to five books and the timeframe of the release, but for me, that never mattered. Sure I wanted the book sooner – but having to wait wasn’t going to stop me from reading the story. The fact that I get five books instead of three, well that’s just a bonus. Although Gideon and Ava reached a place where they overcome a lot, there was still just too much of the story left to be told. I want to know all of those pieces and getting two books gives me a chance to discover them all.<br><br>Now for this installment, it is short in timeframe and we get a few clues as to Gideon’s past – still no clear answers or resolution, but we did get a glimpse into the man himself. Getting a chance to get Gideon’s POV was amazing. I melted when he tried to explain how much he loved this woman and adored seeing him completely fall apart. As much as he wants Ava to just accept things the way they are and move forward, you can clearly see just how damaged he remains, why it is still so important for her to get him to a place where he can accept his past and gain closure.<br><br>As for Ava. Well she sort of pissed me of a bit at the start of the series. Her hang up on closure with Brett was driving me insane. I wanted to slap some sense into her. But even Ava has some growth that needed to be made. Closing the door on her past allowed her to hold a little tighter to her future. Realizing that her relationship with Gideon wasn’t falling into the same patterns of the past, but breaking free of those choices. <br><br>I loved this book, part two still remains my favorite of the series – but this one showcased the characters perfectly. Setting up the conclusion of the story, showing you just how broken Gideon is and just how much he’s willing to give to ensure that he can keep the woman he loves. And the alpha-moments.... fucking swoon. We got pure caveman style Gideon and it was heaven. <br><br><br><br><br><br><br>=================<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420737ra/834946.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Although the wait for this book is going to kill me, I am very happy about this series extending. Book 3 was only a few weeks worth of time and cramming a HEA into a few extra pages would have ruined the feel of the story. A 5th may stretch it a bit, but that all depends on how book 4 goes.<br><br>So many seem unhappy to get more Gideon...*SMH*<br><br>If we can get answers to the new questions that came up in book 3, possibly some resolution to issues discovered in books 1 &amp; 2 and get closer to a more secured HEA for Eva &amp; Gideon...all the better.<br><br>Sylvia Day's writing style is fanfuckingtastic so I have no fear that her adding to the series will do anything to harm it.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393650ra/757896.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420737ra/834947.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15215193831317909608" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qfSzSnCewrk3lYGpFfq1fIX1h33xAB+zgVGiW+f22/qT0tqYy8AL0ZC+NcjiD7+jU6pgtT+NkdTaL+TqKrUpYA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6jKkBuNo5ItY5jbCdxOpl+s9NgcAjL8wz6zw7cb+6inQFM3UWDYt4//NgqOA5qNIPWLRz84BMVeU0rZcC70Ysw==')})
  }

Gideon is the mirror that reflects all my flaws ... and all the beauty I couldn\'t see. He has given me everything. Now, I must prove I can be the rock, the shelter for him that he is for me. Together, we could stand against those who work so viciously to come between us.\n\nBut our greatest battle may lie within the very vows that give us strength. Committing to love was only the beginning. Fighting for it will either set us free ... or break us apart.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"8655082087761455315\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
